Accessibility digest

Synopsis
PageWellTower partner ProMedica Senior Care

Requesterpool@jpdev.pro

Score1456
Tested byTestaro, procedure ts24
Scored byTestilo, procedure tsp24
Digested byTestilo, procedure tdp24

Introduction

This is a digest of results from a battery of accessibility Tests.

The battery includes 1353 automated accessibility tests drawn from ten different packages: Alfa, Axe, Continuum, Equal Access, HTML CodeSniffer, Nu Html Checker, QualWeb, Tenon, Testaro, and WAVE.

These tests were run on the web page named above and gave the page a score of 1456, where 0 would be perfect.

Issue summary

Special issues

log: Score 406. This is based on the amount of browser error logging and miscellaneous logging during the tests.

preventions: Score 100. This is based on tests that the page did not allow to be run. That impedes accessibility progress and risks interfering with tools that users with disabilities need.

solos: Score 20. This is based on issues reported by unclassified tests. Details are in the report.

Classified issues

Issue focusIndication

WCAG: 2.4.7

Score: 168

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package testaro, test focInd, score 148 (Focused element displays no or a nostandard focus indicator)
  • Package alfa, test r65, score 46 (Element in the sequential focus order has no visible focus)

Issue leadingClipsText

WCAG: 1.4.8

Score: 62

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package tenon, test 144, score 60 (Line height is insufficent to properly display the computed font size)

WCAG: 1.4.6

Score: 58

Issue reports in this category:

  • Package axe, test color-contrast-enhanced, score 24 (Element has insufficient color contrast (Level AAA))
  • Package htmlcs, test e:AAA.1_4_6.G17.Fail, score 24 (Text has insufficient contrast)
